# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repositories (version-pinned mirrors):**

- `github.com/sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/grafana-mimir` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/grafana-mimir$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/grafana-loki` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/grafana-loki$` filter

Scope ALL keyword_search/nls_search queries to these repos.
Use the repo name as the `repo` parameter for read_file/go_to_definition/find_references.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

---

**Sourcegraph Repositories:** `github.com/sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec`, `github.com/sg-evals/grafana-mimir`, `github.com/sg-evals/grafana-loki`

## Your Task

71-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've created a comprehensive answer that traces the Prometheus alertmanager notification pipeline in Grafana Mimir. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Key Components in the Pipeline:

1. **Alert Ingestion** - `vendor/github.com/prometheus/alertmanager/api/v2/api.go::postAlertsHandler`
   - HTTP endpoint receives and validates alerts

2. **Alert Storage** - `vendor/github.com/prometheus/alertmanager/provider/mem/alerts.go`
   - In-memory provider stores alerts

3. **Dispatcher** - `vendor/github.com/prometheus/alertmanager/dispatch/dispatch.go`
   - Processes alerts and creates aggregation groups

4. **Routing Tree Traversal** - `vendor/github.com/prometheus/alertmanager/dispatch/route.go::Route.Match()`
   - Matches alerts against routing tree using label matchers

5. **Notification Pipeline Stages** - `vendor/github.com/prometheus/alertmanager/notify/notify.go`
   - Executes silencing, inhibition, time intervals, and routing

6. **Silence Check** - `vendor/github.com/prometheus/alertmanager/silence/silence.go::Silencer`
   - Mutes alerts based on active silences

7. **Inhibition Check** - `vendor/github.com/prometheus/alertmanager/inhibit/inhibit.go::Inhibitor`
   - Suppresses alerts based on inhibition rules

8. **Notifier Dispatch** - `vendor/github.com/grafana/alerting/notify/grafana_alertmanager.go::createReceiverStage()`
   - Creates integration-specific notification stages (dedup, retry, etc.)

9. **Mimir Wrapper** - `pkg/alertmanager/alertmanager.go::Alertmanager`
   - Manages per-tenant alertmanager with state persistence and replication

The complete answer has been written to `/workspace/answer.json` with all files, symbols, and the execution chain through the notification pipeline.

Alert Ingestion\\n**Entry Point**: `vendor/github.com/prometheus/alertmanager/api/v2/api.go::postAlertsHandler`\\n- HTTP POST handler at `/api/v2/alerts` receives incoming alerts\\n- Converts PostableAlerts to internal Alert types with validation\\n- Calls `api.alerts.Put()` to store alerts in the provider\\n\\n### 2. Alert Storage Provider\\n**File**: `vendor/github.com/prometheus/alertmanager/provider/mem/alerts.go`\\n- In-memory alert storage that implements the `provider.Alerts` interface\\n- Stores alerts and notifies subscribers through channels\\n- Dispatcher subscribes to receive alert updates\\n\\n### 3. Dispatcher and Alert Processing\\n**File**: `vendor/github.com/prometheus/alertmanager/dispatch/dispatch.go`\\n- `Dispatcher` class is the core alert processing component\\n- `Run()` method starts the dispatcher, subscribing to alert updates\\n- Receives alerts from the provider and processes them sequentially\\n- For each alert, extracts group labels and creates/updates aggregation groups\\n\\n### 4. Routing Tree Traversal\\n**File**: `vendor/github.com/prometheus/alertmanager/dispatch/route.go`\\n- `Route` class implements the routing tree\\n- `Route.Match(alert.Labels)` performs depth-first, left-to-right search through routing tree\\n- Returns all matching routes for an alert based on label matchers\\n- Respects the `Continue` flag to determine if sibling routes should be evaluated\\n\\n### 5. Notification Pipeline Stages\\n**File**: `vendor/github.com/prometheus/alertmanager/notify/notify.go`\\n- Pipeline executes as a series of stages: `Stage` interface\\n- Each stage can modify alerts or context before passing to next stage\\n- Pipeline order in `GrafanaAlertmanager.ApplyConfig()` (line 745):\\n  1. GossipSettleStage (mesh settling)\\n  2. SilencingStage (silence check)\\n  3. TimeActiveStage (time interval active check)\\n  4. TimeMuteStage (mute time interval check)\\n  5. InhibitionStage (inhibition check)\\n  6. RoutingStage (route-specific receivers)\\n  7. Integration-specific stages (dedup, retry, notification logging)\\n\\n### 6. Silence Check\\n**File**: `vendor/github.com/prometheus/alertmanager/silence/silence.go`\\n- `Silencer` class implements the `Muter` interface\\n- Bound to `silence.Silences` which stores silence rules\\n- `Mutes(ctx, alerts)` checks if alerts match any active silence matchers\\n- Wrapped in `MuteStage` in the notification pipeline\\n\\n### 7. Inhibition Check\\n**File**: `vendor/github.com/prometheus/alertmanager/inhibit/inhibit.go`\\n- `Inhibitor` class implements the `Muter` interface\\n- Evaluates inhibition rules against active alerts\\n- `Mutes(ctx, alerts)` returns true if an alert should be inhibited\\n- Wrapped in `MuteStage` in the notification pipeline\\n- Inhibition rules define which alerts suppress other alerts based on labels\\n\\n### 8. Notifier Dispatch and Integration\\n**File**: `vendor/github.com/grafana/alerting/notify/grafana_alertmanager.go`\\n- `GrafanaAlertmanager` wrapper provides integration management\\n- `ApplyConfig()` method (line 715) constructs the notification pipeline:\\n  - Creates `RoutingStage` (map of receiver names to their stage pipelines)\\n  - For each receiver, creates `FanoutStage` with integration-specific stages\\n- `createReceiverStage()` (line 910) builds the final integration stages:\\n  - WaitStage (cluster peer coordination)\\n  - DedupStage (deduplication based on notification log)\\n  - RetryStage (retry logic for failed notifications)\\n  - SetNotifiesStage (records notification in notification log)\\n  - All wrapped in FanoutStage to execute integrations concurrently\\n\\n### 9. Mimir Alertmanager Wrapper\\n**File**: `pkg/alertmanager/alertmanager.go`\\n- `Alertmanager` class wraps alertmanager components for single tenant\\n- Manages configuration application, state persistence, and replication\\n- Registers HTTP API endpoints for alert management\\n- Integrates with Mimir's multi-tenancy and cluster coordination\\n\\n### Complete Flow Summary\\n1. Alert arrives at `postAlertsHandler` (api/v2/api.go)\\n2. Alert stored in `Alerts` provider (provider/mem/alerts.go)\\n3. Dispatcher notified of new alert (dispatch/dispatch.go)\\n4. Alert labels matched against routing tree (dispatch/route.go::Match)\\n5. For each matching route, create aggregation group\\n6.
